REMOVE-TAG-FROM-SCENARIO
Remove one or more tags from a specific scenario in a feature file

WHEN TO USE
  Use this command when you need to remove tags from a specific scenario, such as removing @wip after completing work, removing @deprecated before deletion, or cleaning up incorrect tags.

USAGE
  fspec remove-tag-from-scenario <file> <scenario> <tags...>

ARGUMENTS
  <file> (required)
    Feature file path (e.g., spec/features/login.feature)
  <scenario> (required)
    Scenario name exactly as it appears in the feature file (e.g., "Login with valid credentials")
  <tags...> (required)
    One or more tags to remove (e.g., @wip @deprecated) - must include @ symbol

OPTIONS
  No options available

EXAMPLES
  1. Remove single tag from scenario
  $ fspec remove-tag-from-scenario spec/features/login.feature "Login with valid credentials" @wip
  ‚úì Removed tag @wip from scenario "Login with valid credentials"

  2. Remove multiple tags from scenario
  $ fspec remove-tag-from-scenario spec/features/login.feature "Login with valid credentials" @wip @manual
  ‚úì Removed tags @wip, @manual from scenario "Login with valid credentials"

COMMON ERRORS
  ‚úó Scenario not found
    Fix: Ensure scenario name matches exactly (case-sensitive)

  ‚úó Tag not found on scenario
    Fix: Use list-scenario-tags to see current tags on the scenario

RELATED COMMANDS
  fspec add-tag-to-scenario
  fspec list-scenario-tags
  fspec remove-tag-from-feature
  fspec retag

NOTES
  ‚Ä¢ Scenario names are case-sensitive and must match exactly
  ‚Ä¢ Tags must include the @ symbol
  ‚Ä¢ Removing a tag that does not exist on the scenario will show an error
  ‚Ä¢ Feature file is automatically reformatted after tag removal

LIST-WORK-UNITS
List work units with optional filtering by status, prefix, or epic

WHEN TO USE
  Use this command when you need to view work units in the backlog, see what's in progress, or filter by specific criteria like status, prefix, or epic.

USAGE
  fspec list-work-units [options]

OPTIONS
  -s, --status <status>
    Filter by workflow status: backlog, specifying, testing, implementing, validating, done, blocked
  --prefix <prefix>
    Filter by work unit prefix (e.g., AUTH, UI, API)
  --epic <epic>
    Filter by epic name

TYPICAL WORKFLOW
  backlog ‚Üí specifying ‚Üí testing ‚Üí implementing ‚Üí validating ‚Üí done. Use --status flag to see work units at each stage.

EXAMPLES
  1. List all work units
  $ fspec list-work-units
  AUTH-001 - User login feature
UI-002 - Dashboard layout

  2. List only backlog items
  $ fspec list-work-units --status=backlog
  AUTH-003 - Password reset
API-004 - User endpoints

  3. List all AUTH-prefixed work units
  $ fspec list-work-units --prefix=AUTH
  AUTH-001 - User login feature
AUTH-003 - Password reset

RELATED COMMANDS
  fspec show-work-unit
  fspec create-story
  fspec create-bug
  fspec create-task
  fspec update-work-unit-status
  fspec board

[90mstdout[2m | src/utils/__tests__/help-interceptor.test.ts[2m > [22m[2mFeature: Scalable help system for all commands[2m > [22m[2mScenario: Handle main program help without command[2m > [22m[2mshould display custom main help with command help note
[22m[39m
fspec - Feature Specification & Project Management for AI Agents
USAGE
  fspec [command] [options]

COMMAND GROUPS
  Use fspec help <group> for detailed help on a specific area:

  specs     - Write and manage Gherkin feature files (create, edit, validate)
  work      - Track work units through ACDD workflow (Kanban, dependencies, board)
  discovery - Collaborative discovery with example mapping (questions, rules, examples)
  metrics   - Track progress and quality (estimates, metrics, reports, statistics)
  setup     - Configure project structure (tags, epics, prefixes, foundation docs)
  hooks     - Lifecycle hooks for workflow automation (validate, add, remove, list)

QUICK START
  fspec init                  - Initialize /fspec slash command for Claude Code
  fspec configure-tools       - Configure test and quality check commands (required)
  fspec validate              - Validate all Gherkin feature files
  fspec create-feature NAME   - Create a new feature file
  fspec list-features         - List all feature files
  fspec check                 - Run all validation checks
  fspec reverse              - Interactive reverse ACDD for existing codebases

GET HELP
  fspec --help            - Show this help
  fspec <command> --help  - Get detailed help for any command
  fspec help specs        - Gherkin feature file commands
  fspec help work         - Work unit and Kanban workflow commands
  fspec help discovery    - Example mapping commands
  fspec help metrics      - Progress tracking and reporting commands
  fspec help setup        - Configuration and setup commands
  fspec help hooks        - Lifecycle hook commands

EXAMPLES
  # Validate specific feature file
  $ fspec validate spec/features/login.feature

  # Filter features by tag
  $ fspec list-features --tag=@critical

  # Add scenario to feature
  $ fspec add-scenario user-authentication "Login with valid credentials"

  # Query scenarios by tags
  $ fspec get-scenarios --tag=@critical --tag=@critical --format=json

DOCUMENTATION
  GitHub: https://github.com/sengac/fspec
  README: See README.md for detailed usage examples
